msg:The government reception hotel is a local five-star hotel with a grand appearance. The guest room facilities are not new but clean and tidy. Overall, it should be good in a fourth-tier city. Let's talk about the bad points ğŸ˜…
The service awareness is not strong. Whether it is the front desk, lobby, or room attendants, they will not take the initiative to say hello and have no smile. The doorman stood stupidly at the door and didn't know to take the initiative to open the car door for the guests.
The service ability is not enough. There are few varieties of Western food in the breakfast restaurant, and there is butter but no butter knife. It is not early to open the door at 7 o'clock, but until 7:30, the stools are still dragged and the tables are tidied, and the noise affects the guests' dining; the sanitation of the restaurant needs to be improved; there is a square across the road from the hotel, and the square dance is opened on time every night, and the sound is particularly loud until 10 o'clock. One song is looped for 1 hour, which is annoying and unfriendly to the guests staying in the hotel.

Finally, Anyang is a tourist city that is about to be and is currently popular. I hope that the service industry can improve itself and seize this great opportunity.

posted:Posted April 8, 2024
msg:It feels good to take my daughter to Anyang, the ancient capital of seven dynasties, during this Qingming holiday. I came here with a backpack in November 2006. There are tall buildings and wide roads along the way from Anyang East High-speed Railway Station to Anyang Guest House. The changes are so great that I thought it was Beijing or Shanghai.

This trip chose the five-star Anyang Guest House, and it turned out to be a correct choice. I ordered the guest house for three nights on Ctrip, which was a 50-55 square meter executive room (there was no price increase during the Qingming holiday), and the hotel upgraded it to a 60-65 square meter executive suite for free. The hotel also provides free pick-up and drop-off service, and the concierge manager Zhang Zhengchao came to the exit of the high-speed railway station to meet us.

The hotel also had a surprise when checking in, with a set of toiletries (which I could use when I went to Iran), drinks, white fungus soup, and a hand-painted tourist map of Anyang. There was a fruit plate in the room every day, and a foot bath bucket and medicine bag were delivered at night (you know, it is very tiring to walk through the Yinxu ruins and the new museum). This series of services is really good, and it is understandable why they have a high score of 4.8 on Ctrip. The picture was taken from the window of my room 2315. The artificial lake in the picture is also part of the hotel. I strongly recommend staying here if you come to Anyang.

msg:I have always stayed in luxury five-star hotels in major cities. When I came to Anyang, I saw that the two five-star hotels on the list were both built in 2014 and 2015. I was really nervous! I came by train and rented a car in Anyang. I booked Wanda at first. I saw online reviews saying that Wanda was difficult to park and charged. This hotel was easy to park and could pick us up at the station. I decisively changed to this Yingbin Hotel. The result was unexpectedly good! Free train station pick-up and drop-off, directly helped us upgrade to three suites for free, arranged various snacks, and all requests were met. The general manager patrolled the lobby at various times every day. I thought he was the lobby manager at first. On the last day, he knew that we were leaving at 7 o'clock in the morning, and he specially sent us off in the lobby early in the morning! There was no one on duty for the 7 o'clock station in the morning, and the staff also got up specially to send us off! In short, it was full of sincerity! Yingbin Hotel definitely deserves five-star praise! The Yinxu Museum was not open this time, and we didn't have time to go to the Red Flag Canal. I plan to stay in Yingbin Hotel next time I come to Anyang!
